Other Regions 175

(Liverpool) Spot sales were good last week. Futures were entirely dominated by global economic difficulties. However, in terms of business, except for the rise in silver prices, which caused slight speculation, all transactions were inter-dealer trades. The amount of short covering, purchases of new cotton by the Bombay gang, and purchases by peers had no impact and instead tended to increase prices. Egyptian cotton became more active, and all sales were absorbed by peers.

Flour Prices Surge Due to Heavy Cash Withdrawals by Various Gangs This Month

丨Australian Wheat Set for Four Vessels, Canadian Wheat for Two Batches丨

Yesterday, the flour market was driven up by the Dalian gang's search for cash after the market opened in the morning. Subsequently, various factories and firms, as well as factories in Shanghai and other places, set prices for four vessels of Australian wheat and two batches of Canadian wheat. (Australian wheat for January delivery was priced at 3 liang, 4 qian, 3 fen, and a half, and then at 3 liang, 4 qian, and a half. April delivery was priced at 3 liang and 4 qian. Canadian wheat, No. 3 for near-term delivery, was priced at 3 liang, 4 qian, and 7 fen and a half, and No. 2 for distant-term delivery was priced at 3 liang, 4 qian, and 8 fen.) The market only then returned to normal. However, due to the heavy cash withdrawals of flour by various gangs this month, the market continued to rise. The red cash withdrawals by Fufeng and small-to-medium-sized factories have reached 2 liang and 1 fen and around 2 liang, respectively. Fuxin is short of cash and is offering 50,000 bags for delivery in three weeks, priced at 1 liang, 9 qian, 7 fen, and a half net. Therefore, public sentiment and market conditions are good. The closing price for this month continued to rise by 1 fen and a half. Prices for January and beyond initially rose and then leveled off, with the closing price for January up 2.5 fen, February and March up 5 li, and April and May up 2.5 li.

Merchants Still Actively Hoarding Early Rice

Yesterday, there was a lack of rice on the market, and early rice was very popular because merchants were very active in hoarding it and continued to buy Jiangxi machine-milled late rice. Yesterday, they also resumed buying Hunan machine-milled oil rice. Both the Quanzhou and Fuzhou routes of the Fujian gang were also very interested. The North China gang had some dealings, but the merchants were most active in hoarding it, and the market looked good, with prices rising by about one jiao. Over 5,000 bags were offered on the market, and merchants bought more than half of them. Most of the early rice was sold to Fujian province, with little going to North China. It is estimated that 1,500 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled late rice were offered, priced at 8 yuan and 6 jiao to 8 yuan and 2 jiao, as well as 50 bags of machine-milled red rice, priced at 7 yuan and 9 jiao and a half. 2,300 bags of Hunan machine-milled oil rice were offered, priced at 8 yuan and 7 jiao and a half to 6 jiao, as well as 1,300 bags of machine-milled red rice, priced at 8 yuan and 1 jiao and a half to 7 yuan and 9 jiao and a half, and 200 bags of polished red rice, priced at 8 yuan and 9 jiao to 8 jiao and a half, and 40 bags of polished Jing rice, priced at 7 yuan and 1 jiao.

Chicago Wheat Rises Slightly

On Saturday last week (the 17th), Chicago wheat initially fell due to sales from the East, but then rose due to the strength of Winnipeg wheat. The trading volume on the 16th totaled 30 million bushels. The market prices for the 17th are listed on the left:

Sugar Market: Over Two Thousand Bags of Raw and Red Sugar Offered

丨Price at Thirteen Liang and a Half丨

Yesterday, the sugar market saw little fluctuation in the standard gold price, and the trend gradually stabilized. The Guild set the price of No. 24 coarse white sand high-grade goods at 15 liang, 5 qian, 2 fen, and a half, and ordinary goods at 15 liang, 4 qian, 7 fen, and a half, with over 600 bags traded. No. 18 medium white sand and Nos. 89 and 90 Dutch red sugar remained unchanged. Xin Chaoqing (sugar) could not be uniformly priced by various firms, and as it was being replaced by new sugar, it was difficult to keep it off the market for long. Therefore, most of it has been offered on the market in recent days, priced at 9 liang and 1 qian to 8 liang and 3 qian, with fluctuations of four to five qian compared to the previous price. On the foreign firm side, Wah Shing offered over 2,000 bags of raw and red sugar, priced at 13 liang and a half. Jian Gang offered twenty to thirty boxes of standard Five Blessings white rock candy, priced at 11 liang per box, and miscellaneous brands were priced at 10 liang and 3 qian. The market is stable.

Also, according to a telegram from New York on the 17th, the spot price of sugar is 8.125 cents, and the futures prices for December, January, and September are unchanged, while the futures prices for March, May, and July are all up by one pound. Also, according to a telegram from London, the December futures price is up by a small halfpenny, the March futures price is up by a small quarterpenny, and the May futures price is unchanged. Also, according to a telegram from Java, white sugar is still priced at 8 shillings and one and a half pence (120 pounds).

Dried Southern and Northern Goods: Longan Bubble Prices Decline

There have been no recent shipments of large-bubble longans from Quanzhou. However, the previous shipments have already been mostly sold. Since last month, sales have been very sluggish. Therefore, various firms are taking a wait-and-see approach and have no intention of buying. The firms also have higher costs and are unwilling to sell at low prices. However, after a long period of being kept off the market, sales have not improved. Firms are now reducing prices on the previously high-priced goods to try to sell them. Therefore, the market situation is even more depressed. It was heard yesterday that some of the goods had already been sold off, with prices falling by about three liang compared to before. The remaining goods will also be sold off in the coming days. The market situation is unlikely to improve within the year, as inventories are too full.

Hardware: New Iron Wire Has Arrived

After the gangs in Wenzhou and Hankou bought large quantities of new iron wire, the market ran out of stock. There has been no news of it on the market for months. Yesterday, it was heard that Gonghexing has received 250 barrels of new goods, which were ordered by hardware stores along North Suzhou Road. Many deals have already been made with customers. The price for Nos. 16 to 20 is 13 liang per dan, and Nos. 21 to 25 are estimated at 13 liang and 7 qian and a half. It is said that over 50 barrels have been offered on the market.

Steel Pricing Eased Yesterday

Yesterday's news from foreign firms said that overseas steel prices have softened recently due to tighter foreign exchange rates. Steel products have fallen by half a pound per ton, and iron products have fallen by two to three shillings.

According to a Reuters dispatch from London, black iron sheets (3X6 bundles of 13 sheets) are priced at £10 15s, galvanized iron sheets are priced at £10 per ton, tinplate (20 inches X 1420) of 112 sheets per hundred pounds is priced at 16 shillings and one and a half pence. Bismuth and antimony (Chinese) have risen slightly to £18 10s per ton.

Free Talk

Lotus Ballad (1)

— Mu Shiying

Drifting, like yellow leaves in autumn, over one mountain after another, one river after another – we are two people.

Together with a pair of sandalwood clappers and a Chinese fiddle, we travel from this city to that city. In front of thatched cottages, in front of the black-lacquered gates of palaces, in the streets, in the examination halls, we sing the Lotus Ballad, begging for a copper, a cup of soup, a bowl of cold rice – we are two people.

Yes, we are two people, but she died yesterday.

It was twenty years ago, when my hair was as black as my pupils. The soldiers bombed my home. The family members died, ran away, no one knew where they went. I ran south alone, and I was really tired when I ran until evening, so I ran to the gazebo in front. It was there that I met her. She was inside, sitting on the ground crying, sobbing. I was still shy at that time, so I sat down a little further away. She secretly glanced at me, and her crying became softer. I thought to myself... I should comfort her. Why is this girl crying here alone?

"Don't cry, girl! What are you crying about?" I said to her from afar.

She didn't say anything and just cried, even louder. Wasn't this a mess? I didn't dare to speak any more. I looked outside the gazebo, not daring to look at her. It was getting dark, and a crescent moon was shining on the fields. Near and far, I couldn't find any fire. A dog was standing outside the gazebo, looking at me. I remember it was a black dog. We also had a black dog at home. Our ox was yellow, and there was also a black chicken with beautiful long feathers. I wanted to kill it for three years, but I couldn't bear to. We also had a tabby cat. My younger sister loved that cat very much, but my father hated it, saying it loved to steal food. But my mother loved my younger sister, and my father loved me. When the tabby cat stole something, my father wanted to chop off its head, but my younger sister held it tightly and wouldn't let go, so my father hit her. Whenever I heard her crying, he would hit me. As soon as I cried, my father and mother would start arguing. But where did my father go? Where did my mother and younger sister go? And what about that black dog, that yellow ox, that tabby cat? Where did they go?

As I thought about it, I also wanted to cry, but she had stopped crying at some point. I turned my head to look, and she quickly turned her head away, afraid of being embarrassed and not letting me see her face. So I looked at her from behind. She was eating something there, eating it quite sweetly. Gulp, I swallowed a mouthful of saliva, and it sounded like thunder in the middle of the night. She turned her head to look, and I don't know why I gulped down another mouthful of saliva. She chuckled. I was so embarrassed. She took out a something and held it out from afar. I couldn't care about being embarrassed, and I ran over with a red face to eat it. I also didn't dare to speak. After I finished eating, I watched her eat. She still had five. When she raised her head, I quickly turned my eyes to the side. But she gave me another one. My face was really red and hot.

"Thank you," I said.

After I finished eating, she gave me two more.

"Thank you so much," I said.

"Want more?"

How could I say that it wasn't enough? I said it was enough.

General Han's Smile

— Gao Ming

A while ago, we saw in the newspaper that in Linqu County, Shandong Province, there were bandit leaders Li Lechuan, Song Wangshi, and tailor Fu Baoqi, who called themselves the Heavenly Emperor, Earthly Emperor, and Human Emperor, and prepared to ascend the throne next March. They were caught by the authorities. It's not surprising for a Chinese person to harbor a bit of wishful thinking. The bigger hope is to win the two or three hundred thousand yuan jackpot with ten dollars in horse racing, and the smaller hope is to turn one copper coin into an orange or a candy figure. This is what we are used to seeing, and no one is surprised. Therefore, we don't want to blame Mr. Li Fu and Mrs. Song, but what interests us is what happened afterward.

It wasn't until yesterday that the newspaper gave us a report (see today's newspaper):

"Han Fuju interrogated the false Song Wangshi at 8 p.m. tonight in the provincial government office. Song Wangshi's confession was mostly gibberish, vaguely saying... Lord Han, please guarantee that I will be Emperor, and if not, cut me into eight pieces. Han Da didn't dare... Han pitied Mrs. Song Wang because she was stimulated and had a nervous breakdown, and ordered Li to go home and be at peace, and advised others not to believe in Christianity. Li Lechuan and Fu Baoqi, Zhi Huaqing, were released at the same time, along with the divine ox, the divine building, and the imperial carriage. (Jinan Special Dispatch, 18th)"

Mrs. Song and Mr. Li Fu were so carefully cared for by General Han this time, which surprised us, but what we want to study now is General Han's smile.

According to experts, there are seven types of smiles:

1. Physiological smiles, such as tickle-induced smiles, and the silly smiles of babies; 2. Sad smiles; 3. Angry smiles; 4. Sick smiles, the hysterical laughter of the mentally ill; 5. Humorous smiles; 6. Deceptive smiles; 7. Joyful smiles.

We don't know what kind of smile General Han's smile is.

The Sanxian Player

— Jiang Tianwei

It's late at night. The street is pitch black. There are no streetlights and no pedestrians. Three or five stars flicker with faint light in the sky. It’s a narrow street, and the shops on both sides are like two walls. The street is full of filth, forever permeated with a kind of stench.

In this late night, every day I hear a sanxian player, playing the sanxian, slowly walking from one end of the street to the other. On this long street, he always walks back and forth. The sound of the sanxian is always sadly echoing.

This sanxian player has been playing back and forth on the street seven times already. From his sanxian, I know that he is anxious, and a kind of resentful emotion controls the movement of his hands. First, he plays a happy tune, like a carefree person, with laughter in the sound, like wanton tears. Then, he plays a melancholy tune, dull, desolate, like the weeping of a widow. At this time, he has already passed this street for the fourth time.

The night is getting deeper, but he is still playing the sanxian, slowly walking across the street. On the three strings, he is telling of his resentment, the sadness of his life, the lack of compassion in the world. The sound is like a rushing stream in the mountains, the tears of the waves in the sea, the low weeping of a widow in the late night, the groaning of wounded soldiers on the battlefield.

I listened quietly, feeling that the sanxian player's heart was deeply carved with the marks of life's suffering. He must truly understand the world. The sound of the sanxian came from afar again. I couldn't help but open the door, walk to the street, and invite the sanxian player into my living room. He was blind, his face full of wind and dust, reflecting a sad shadow. He was playing day and night. I asked him with a sympathetic tone:

"Don't you feel lonely playing like this in the late night?"

"Lonely! Sir! We blind people don't know what loneliness is."

"The sound of your sanxian tells me... Alas! I sympathize with you!"

"Sympathize with me! Sir! Thank you! Although we are said to be blind, I am a wanderer who plays three strings. I have tasted the bitterness of wind and rain, the terror of having no food or drink and running out of food. I am... but I don't forget that I play the sanxian. This is my life..."

"I think you can get the sympathy of people, right!"

"I don't want sympathy. I play the sanxian and walk through the streets and alleys. Ruthless children throw stones at me, arrogant dogs bite me."

Many people spit on me, laugh at me, and tease me. Where is the sympathy? I don't want it! I play the sanxian, telling of the injustices of the world."

"......"

The sanxian player heard that I was silent, so he plucked the sanxian, a few low sounds, gradually getting higher. An oil lamp in the living room radiated a dim light, and the sound of the sanxian trembled.

I couldn't stand it any longer. The sound of this desolate sanxian broke my heart. I gently stuffed fifty copper coins into his hand. He stopped playing the sanxian in surprise, and seemed to say with emotion:

"I haven't told your fortune, sir, but I'm receiving your money. I shouldn't. I can't receive this..."

"................"

"I can't! If I receive this kind of alms, the sanxian will break. Alas! I can't!"

What could I say? As expected, the sanxian player did not accept this extra kindness from me. He seemed to be frightened.

The next night, I didn't hear the sound of the sanxian trembling in the street. I thought he was sick. I didn't hear it the third night either. The fourth day, the fifth day... it was gone forever. Where did this sanxian player go?

I regret it very much. My compassionate heart has driven the blind man on an even longer journey.

My heart will forever remember the sanxian player.

My Cherished Younger Sister

— Ms. Biyao

3. Ailing Fallen Blossom

Luo Ying grew up by the lakeside of Taihu, with bright eyes and pearly teeth, lively and graceful. As for her writing, it was even more enchanting and delicate, with twists, turns, and youthful beauty. From Hangzhou to Shanghai, after several years of schooling, she completed the prototype of a modern woman; in thought and deed, she could liberate herself. Once, she was disgusted with the school she was in, and deliberately, on that week's life report card, wrote that the most unsatisfactory thing this week was the breaking of her hymen. This paper was handed to the training department, causing a great uproar, and she was immediately expelled. In fact, at that time, she knew nothing except for some gender knowledge taught by the physiology teacher in class. However, she hated those hypocritical male teachers who pretended to be monks and nuns on the surface, but secretly were not to be questioned, so she deliberately made a joke. Later, she applied to a school, and because her paper was outstanding, the result of the first written test ranked her at the top. However, in the second oral test, a single female teacher saw that she was too lively, and asked her if she had a boyfriend. She immediately replied that she did. Then she asked her where her boyfriend was now? (The meaning was that if he was far away, it wouldn't be too important). She replied that she had more than one boyfriend, and they were everywhere. The female teacher was so stunned that she couldn't ask any more questions, just stared at her blankly for a long time, waved her hand and told her to leave; so she failed the exam. At a speech competition at a university in Shanghai, she met a young man. She immediately wrote him a letter, pursued him, and automatically developed all aspects of love. Sometimes on Sundays, when she returned to school from outside, friends asked her where she came from, and she honestly said she came from a hotel. If anyone sneered, she would scold them for being vulgar. Her [life] was not vulgar at all. All hypocritical, apprehensive, timid, and rigid words and deeds were completely absent. With her bold and outstanding spirit, she could create, fight, and inspire the cowardly and warn the stubborn. Unfortunately, her life in the last two years was too irregular, indulging in excessive drinking and eating, and unrestrained pleasure. On the one hand, she contracted a lung disease from her lover, and on the other hand, she suffered a loss of vitality due to a careless abortion. Recently, she has become emaciated and has been abandoned by her admirers, lying alone in illness in a foreign land. That haggard face is unrecognizable. Her studies have been interrupted, and it is unknown how long her life can last. All her friends sigh when they talk about her.

New Scientific Weapons (2)

— Yi

The second terrible weapon is the electric cannon. This cannon does not use gunpowder, but completely uses the power of electricity to launch projectiles. It was invented by the Frenchman Fuxiong Bipler in 1916. Originally, the impact distance of a cannon was directly proportional to the speed of the projectile when it flew out of the muzzle; now, it can launch a one-hundred-kilogram projectile at a speed of 4,000 meters per second, with an impact distance of eight hundred kilometers.

If this becomes a reality, then in the next world war, France's enemies can safely bombard Paris from distant rear positions. Previously, the German army's self-proclaimed unparalleled Bertha gun had a range of only one hundred and twenty kilometers, which is nothing compared to the power of the electric cannon. Although the manufacturing cost of electric cannons is very high, in theory and in practice, their performance is very good; however, further research is still needed, and when they can be practically applied, they will not appear on the battlefield. Sitting in Paris, you can use cannons to bombard Berlin, London, and Rome. This may not necessarily be a futuristic dream of the twenty-first century, and may appear in the near future.

A Long Creative Work

Crossroads of the Era and Love 20

— Zhang Ziping

Which side should I go to? Which side is more important? The Ren family's appointment cannot be changed. Should I ask Yaoxing to change the date? Earlier or later would be fine, as long as it's not the afternoon of the 5th.]

He felt that no matter what, he couldn't sacrifice the Ren family's dinner. This wasn't just about the dinner itself, but he wanted to see Ms. Liu Peizhen, Mrs. Ren, who had given him a very good impression since their meeting that day.

Using the index number of the north series, subtract one screen from the original index, which is the differential of the variable.

Professor Wang's old tune was playing again. Haiquan thought that this teacher's teaching method was really not clever. He had no intention of listening to Mr. Wang's lecture, just hoping for the bell to ring and end the class quickly.

He suddenly thought of Mrs. Tsuruko. From Mrs. Tsuruko, he imagined the intimate scene between that Japanese guy and Mrs. Tsuruko. A wave of depression arose again in his mind.

[What's there to be afraid of! I still have a wad of paper in my pocket.]

He reached into his pocket to feel the wad of paper, comforting himself, wanting to take it out and look at it, but worried that the classmate Zhu sitting behind him would peek.

He finally endured four hours, and the clock struck twelve. In the afternoon, there was only one hour of military training, and he was unwilling to stay in this dry and tasteless school any longer.

Subjectively, he really didn't want to go back to the public residence, but the objective environment forced him to take that road.

Sitting on the tram, he unfolded the wad of paper that Ms. Zhuo had tossed him.

[Haiquan, my home address is No. 15, Lane S, H Road, North Sichuan Road. I have important matters to discuss with you. Please come to my residence around 8 o'clock tonight. Please do not refuse.]

He really couldn't figure out why Zhuo Shuhua wanted him to go to her house. He just thought, I'll go see her. Returning to the entrance of the Zeng Public Residence, he listened intently to the temple side, it was quiet and still, without any sound. He had expected Mrs. Tsuruko to be standing at the entrance to welcome him. But looking at the current situation, he was disappointed. He pushed the back door hard, and there was no [lock] inside. The door opened at his push. The maid heard the sound and walked out of the front parlor rubbing her eyes.

[Mr. Lin, you're back so early?]

[Where is the young mistress?]

Haiquan couldn't help but ask her this.

[She went out with that Japanese gentleman this morning.]

[Just the two of them?]

[And that beautiful Japanese girl.]

Hearing the maid's words, Haiquan thought of the beautiful Japanese girl about fifteen or sixteen years old he saw standing behind Mrs. Tsuruko this morning.

[Mr. Lin hasn't eaten yet, has he? The young mistress prepared Mr. Lin's snacks before she went out.] After hearing this, Haiquan secretly thanked Mrs. Tsuruko in his heart. He returned to his room on the third floor and sat for a while, then the maid brought him a large bowl of mushroom and chicken noodles to eat.

Supplement to the Local News of Shen Bao

Random Thoughts

Dotting and Circling

— Fo

Recently, the Random Thoughts section of this publication has abandoned the new punctuation and has actually started using dotting and circling. Dotting and circling was a favorite trick of essayists in the past, used for things like "great opening and great closure" or "vigorous and unrestrained," using large circles for emphasis. Now, these fart-like Random Thoughts (it should be stated here that this refers to my own Random Thoughts; other people's Random Thoughts are the exception), what is there to circle? It's truly a performance of Shen Bao's sixty-year-old virgin. Her attitude, trying to appear charming and beautiful, adorned with jewels and jade, with three-inch golden lilies and embroidered sleeves. ["Having seen thousands of women, I've never seen such a delightful maiden before,"] but ultimately it lacks contemporaneity. The general feudal coloration feels too strong, and it definitely cannot compete with several ["modern misses"]. Truly, Random Thoughts will not compete with several modern misses in long cheongsams and short overcoats. Nor dare it compete with modern misses; adding some dotting and circling is just a curious concept of ["not discarding what I take"] and ["waste utilization"]. ["A leper's son looks good to his own eyes,"] I am also human, and naturally cannot escape this common mentality. Therefore, even if anyone scolds my writing as extremely bad or incomprehensible, although I dare not be presumptuous, belittle myself, or willingly submit, I will also never ["value my worn-out broom as if it were gold"] or self-importantly ["recite with three sighs"] or slap the table and shout "bravo." Nor will I dare to boast about myself, claiming to be some ancient writer or some new literary figure, or that my work is earth-shatteringly amazing.

Mr. Chen Leng once said that writing articles is like excreting waste; after excreting, one should never turn back to look at it, whether it is hard or soft, fragrant or foul. I share the same principle with Mr. Chen; no matter how bad or ugly the fart I release, I will never turn back to look at it. But a pockmarked girl insists on applying rouge and powder, trying to cover up her embroidered face. This is also the common nature of pockmarked girls; hence Yingchuan Chen An once wrote a poem saying, ["Heaven pities her for not being beautiful, and adorns her face with makeup."] But even so, it is nothing more than a theory of glossing over and disguising flaws. This publication's addition of some dotting and circling may also be the intention of a pockmarked young lady to be coy and affected; this is what I dare to admit.

To change the subject, but driving backward is not a good business strategy; for example, a person should always walk forward on a bright road, never turn backward, and become a straggler of the times. Truly, who wants to drive backward, who wants to be a straggler? Indeed, he is an idiot, a fool. But try to open your eyes and look; from the government to society, from the warlords to the police officers standing at the gate, from important people to the "tossing the crown" of the little [third brothers], where doesn't one find examples of driving backward and turning backward? For example, in weddings, there are small ancestral shrines and magnificent military bands, inside there is a high-hanging flag of the party and the nation, and outside there is a pair of ancestral shrine lanterns raised high. These are all common contradictory tricks; what does it matter if we add some dotting and circling?

Moreover, is adding dotting and circling really being a straggler? Is not adding dotting and circling really being modern? Are evolution and regression, outdatedness and modernity, really only distinguished by dotting and circling? If this is truly the case, if it is indeed the case, if the distinction lies in this one point, then why wouldn't I happily hang up a sheep's head and sell dog meat, and pretend to be a modern brand? But the so-called new punctuation is nothing more than imitating Western punctuation. But Western punctuation, which we consider new, has long become outdated in Europe and America, and cannot be said to be an absolutely novel and delightful thing. Furthermore, whether [a seven-and-a-half-inch hat fits perfectly] is also a problem. Saying this any further would be too wordy; it's better to conclude quickly. In short, in modern matters, one cannot thoroughly investigate the roots. Whether it's modern or outdated, just be so-so.

Literature and Art

Feelings

— Yikong

(1)

Long have I glared at the new capital,

Wind and snow stir sorrows vast.

Do swans only scheme for rice grains?

Can Yan Dan buy Jing Ke once more?

Hesitating, I add no flowers' hues,

Solemnly, I listen to leaves' sound.

Ashamed of my youthful silence long,

Let me, from butchering dogs, discern life's course.

(2)

Throughout the divine land, storms arise,

A mass of dragons, wriggling like maggots.

Revolution has melted like morning snow,

Soul-stirring most is the northern wind's arrival.

Still I hear court debates on resisting insult,

Soon I'll see surrender flags raised nationwide.

Undead, this heart cannot but wander,

From mud, I dare cut first to free myself.

(Corresponding Poem)

Science

Method of Making Cotton from Straw

— Yiheng

Cotton is a necessity in the world, naturally produced. Today, in civilized countries around the world, there are people who make it artificially. The raw materials used are discarded by farmers, such as rice straw or mulberry bark, which can all be used for manufacturing. Furthermore, it does not require a large capital investment. The equipment used is available in every household, such as (pots, sieves, buckets, boxes, etc.). The chemical materials used are available in pharmacies and art supply stores everywhere. Now, the method of making cotton from rice straw is described below.

Rice straw: One hundred catties (referring to the clean ones)

Caustic soda (i.e., lye): Nine catties and four ounces

Sulfuric acid (i.e., strong sulfuric acid): One catty, seven maces, and two fen (divided into two applications)

Bleaching powder: Twelve catties and four ounces

(1) First, remove the weeds from the rice straw, use a knife to cut off the roots and ears, peel off the leaves, and cut the middle section into pieces about two or three inches long, preparing them for use. It does not matter whether it is glutinous or non-glutinous rice straw, all can be used. However, it is best to use fresh, white, and tender rice straw from the current year. Old or moldy rice straw must not be used.

(2) Put clean water into a pot and boil it. Add caustic soda (Sodium hydroxide) to the water. After it dissolves, slowly add the rice straw, stir well with a stick, and boil until it is soft.

(3) Scoop out the boiled rice straw, put it in a leaky bamboo basket, rinse with clean water. If there are any undissolved pieces, pick them out and mash them. Put them back in clean water, pick out the moldy grass and grass nodes, and squeeze them dry.

(4) Put cold water in a vat, pour in sulfuric acid (Sulfuric Acid), six ounces and eight fen, to form dilute sulfuric acid, put the straw floss in, soak for a quarter of an hour, take it out, squeeze it dry, and pull it loose.

(5) Dissolve bleaching powder (Bleaching Powder) in clean water, remove the lime, then heat water and stir evenly. Immediately put the squeezed-dry straw floss in, stir evenly with a wooden stick, cover it for a whole day and night, and it will become white grass cotton (Note) If the bleaching lime is not removed, it will not become cotton.

(6) Pour sulfuric acid, ten ounces and six maces and four fen, into a vat of clean water to form extremely dilute sulfuric acid. Wash the bleached straw floss with clean water once, squeeze it dry, put it in sulfuric acid, stir evenly, leave it exposed for one hour to remove the bleach odor, then wash it with clean water, squeeze it dry, put it in the sun, dry it to 70%, pull it apart, and dry it to 100%. It can be fluffed to become clean white cotton.

A Tragic and Stirring Letter

My dearest sister Min;

When I wrote this letter, I didn't want to tell you, but if I don't tell you, I won't have another day to

Page 18

Supplement to the Local News of Shen Bao

say anything! Besides, you will eventually find out sooner or later, so I should tell you!

Since the day I left you at the train station, my heart was filled with the sadness of separation, but when I thought that it was for the honor of the nation and the survival of the country, I felt happy in my heart!

Our volunteer army has been developing in the Northeast! When we arrived at General Ma's command, they were very welcome because we had all received considerable training in school, so a part of us was immediately assigned to the rear defense for security, and another part went to the front line!

At that time, I was also assigned to a team on the front line. When we were about to face the battle, the continuous sound of guns whizzed into our ears. Although we were all young people who had not experienced battle, our blood was boiling, and we did not feel any fear. We just looked around very sharply, preparing for the arrival of the dwarfs!

Early the next morning, the commander of the volunteer army ordered us to be especially careful and vigilant, because we heard that a part of the enemy had transferred from the town to our front. At the same time, they sent more than a dozen brothers with rich war experience to strengthen our defense line.

In the evening, scattered and chaotic gunshots, mixed with the rumbling cannons from behind, continued to fire. Sure enough, several tanks carrying dwarf soldiers rushed into our line. At that time, the commander ordered us to charge, and we bravely went up to resist. The dwarf soldiers all jumped out of the vehicles to fight us in close combat. Although I had been hit by several bullets in my leg, I did not feel it at all at that time. Our courage seemed to be even stronger! As a result, half of the dwarf soldiers died, and the rest mostly fled. However, many of our brothers also died. In this conflict, I also killed several dwarf soldiers, which was really enjoyable!

The enemy reinforced their troops in an instant, and many more came. At this time, our classmate Chen was killed by a dwarf soldier, which added a lot of anger. While we were chasing, there seemed to be planes circling in the sky. Then something fell near us. With a bang, I lost consciousness.

When I woke up, I was lying in the hospital bed, my body full of shrapnel wounds. Sister Min! My right leg was also blown off. The doctor told me to rest assured, I probably won't make it? I am going to die in the shortest amount of time, so I write this letter in pain. Perhaps when you see this letter, I have already left with a smile!

Oh, sister Min! You don't need to be sad for me, I died for the survival of the country and the honor of the nation.

I wish you happiness! My dearest sister Min!

Your loving Kun, written at the wounded soldiers' hospital

The Farmer's Sorrow

— Zhang Yiping

Since graduating, I have been running around in Shanghai and have not returned to my hometown. Currently, I have returned home for two days because of matters concerning the fields. Firewood and farm tools are piled up on the farmyard. The farmers have worked hard for a year, and this is when they can rest. Moreover, this year is also a year of good harvest. I imagined setting up a low table in the farmyard, with the whole family gathering around to eat dinner. Eating from sunset to dark. Perhaps this is their happiest time?

Our village completely preserves the simple customs of the past. For example, if someone has a wedding or funeral, the whole village comes to help, treating each other like family. On the evening I returned home, after dinner, the old man next door, as usual, held a water pipe and a particularly long paper tube, muttering in his mouth as he came to my house to chat. He is an old child. When I was in my hometown before, he would play tug-of-war and catch sparrows with us. Sometimes, he would even buy one or two copper coins' worth of sweets to chew on. Therefore, when I heard his footsteps, I stepped out of the door to invite him in.

The old man did not have the vigor of the past, nor did he have his usual smile. After sitting down in front of the kerosene lamp, he first sighed and suddenly asked me, "Did we lose a lot in this war with the Japanese?"

"Quite a bit. I heard it's several million yuan!"

"It's really not worth it. How can the Chinese beat the Japanese?" The old man said logically. "Young master, you don't know that they are going to build an airfield here. The people in this village are so scared that they have all moved away..." He shook his head and took a puff of smoke.

"The newspapers said it wasn't built!"

"Yes! But thousands of acres of fields here have been ruined! And people's graves have been overturned. Under the Qing Dynasty laws, digging up graves would be punishable by death."

"What will happen to so many fields?"

"Fortunately, the order to withdraw the project came early, and we have now harvested the grain."

"That's good. If we can have a good harvest, then don't worry about so much."

"Young master, the harvest is indeed good, but the price of rice is so cheap, and the landlords (i.e., the landowners) are unwilling to reduce the rent in kind. (It is a custom in the hometown that after the farmers sell the rice, they use the proceeds to pay the rent in kind to the landowners.) What can the people in the countryside do?"

"Old man, do you have your own fields to farm?"

"It's not good to have our own fields either. The grain tax increases year after year. If there is a famine year, what will we use to pay the grain!" He smoked as he spoke, and the particularly long paper tube had only a small section left that he could hold between his fingers. I knew he was about to get up and leave. As expected, he stood up and ended his speech. "It's not good to farm other people's fields, and it's not good to farm our own fields. It's really hard for the people in the countryside!"

A sad mood completely enveloped his wrinkled face.

Regulations for the Shop Clerk Communication Column

(1) Purpose of Communication: This column aims to gather wisdom and benefit each other, interpret difficult problems, sharpen each other, and enhance the happiness of life.

(2) Communication Target: The target of this column is limited to shop clerks and apprentices, and the location is limited to this city.

(3) Communication Content: All aspects of personal daily life, such as:

(1) Occupation (2) Moral and academic cultivation (3) Entertainment and sports (4) Marriage, as well as other issues related to the country and society, are welcome. If the content of the question is too profound and beyond the ability of this column, it can also be referred to this newspaper's [Reader Consultant for answering.

(4) How to Submit Letters:

(1) The name, age, origin, occupation, and detailed mailing address must be clearly stated at the end of the letter; this information must be provided in subsequent letters.

(2) The style of the letter is not limited, but should be simple and easy to understand, and must be clearly written.

(3) Please write the words "Shen Bao Guan, Supplement to the Local News, Shop Clerk Communication Column" on the envelope. If a reply is required, please attach a two-cent stamp.

(4) Communicators must cut out the special stamp published by this column and paste it on the upper left corner of the letter. Letters without the stamp will not be answered.

(5) Handling Method after Receiving Letters:

(1) This newspaper reserves the right to disclose the questions discussed that it deems to have value in contributing to the public in the newspaper.

(2) To respect the opinions of the communicators, all letters that state that they do not wish to disclose their names, or that require individual replies, may be handled accordingly.

(3) If communicators wish to disclose their letters in the newspaper, but cannot disclose the full text due to the length, relevant excerpts will be published. In addition, if the content of the question is complicated and requires careful study, which may lead to delays in answering or disclosing it, please understand. (4) When there are many letters, answers will be provided in the order in which they are received, and we ask for your understanding if there are any delays.

Novel

Writing a Letter to a Friend's Wife (Continued Eleven)

— Qin Shouou

These kinds of jokes, containing so much blood and tears, effortlessly increased the students' attention to the Zhou-Li romance. At the same time, both male and female students were worried about Dajing because the two of them were too different in personality, status, and environment. Dajing's strength was his knowledge, but knowledge was considered worthless by girls in the 19th century. Therefore, the prediction that Dajing would definitely be abandoned by Li Fang had already been definitively concluded by the students.

Dajing had also heard these predictions at that time, especially from me, who, as a good friend, tirelessly—this qualification remained until I met you on Seward Road, when it automatically disappeared—tried to dissuade him. However, he was deeply intoxicated by Li Fang's charming smiles, and naturally treated my words as a passing breeze.

Because he was so deeply infatuated, he was in such pain after the breakup that he felt as if he had lost his soul.

Who would have thought that the soul he lost three years ago would suddenly meet me head-on. But at this time, I was no longer Dajing's good friend, but a bad friend who almost stole his second soul.

[Where is Mr. Zhu working now?] Although I am a very talkative person, I was really not in good spirits that night, and for a long time, I couldn't think of a word to say to her. Instead, she was the first to ask me.

[Um! ...Me? I am...] Unexpectedly, her first question made me unable to answer. If she had asked me the day before, I could have easily told her that I was with Dafeng Foreign Firm; but now, I had resigned from Dafeng's job six hours ago. How could I say I was working there? I hesitated for a long time before making up a lie: [Teaching at University K.]

[Oh! Isn't the president of University K XXX? They originally wanted to invite our Mr. Ma last semester,] My unfounded lie actually opened her floodgates of words. [Because he was already the president of K College and knew that University K was a notoriously poor school, he didn't go. What subject are you teaching there? How long have you been teaching?]

[So, you are now Mrs. Ma Jichuan. My apologies!] I ignored her question and first made a note of the five words [our Mr. Ma] she had said.

She smiled very proudly. But in her pride, there seemed to be some pretense of modesty.

Dear little friend! Don't you always scold me for being the worst villain in the world? You mean it as a joke, but it's actually true! I am not only bad, but also good at guessing other people's thoughts. Li Fang's words and her kind of pretense of modesty turned around a few times in my mind, and I immediately understood the truth of the matter.

[Ma Jichuan's wife is Ms. Ouyang Jinming, who often stays at the YWCA. Li Fang has probably unfortunately become his concubine!] The report after the mind's work.

[Oh! Mrs. Ma! Forgive me, let me ask you a question.] I prepared to seize this opportunity that she presented and make fun of her, to vent some of Dajing's grievances. [When did Dr. Ma divorce Ms. Ouyang, who often works for the YWCA?]

This question really embarrassed her. She immediately lowered her head, pressed her bright red lips against the rim of the glass, and remained silent for a long time, unable to utter a sound. Her face gradually turned red, as if she were drunk.

Her embarrassment further confirmed my mind's report; I was extremely pleased, almost bursting out laughing.

After all, she was a socialite. Although she was caught off guard by my embarrassment, she gradually recovered her composure after five or six minutes. She first flashed her fluent eyes, containing a hint of resentment, at me a few times, and then smiled generously.

Movie Supplement

Rare News from the Film World

Is Sun Bici a Comedian? (Part 1)

— Fulun

Sun Bici's humor makes children clap their hands and laugh when they see her. This is indeed comparable to Chaplin. But whether Sun Su is a comedian is worth discussing. According to a famous director in Hollywood, [They all call Sun Bici to play comedic roles, but they don't know that one of the greatest tragic authors of the era has been buried.]

To know whether Sun Bici is a comedian or a tragedian, please first study her life. There are many things that many people do not know, and I will describe them below.

Sun Su first arrived in Hollywood more than thirteen or four years ago. At that time, she was as lonely as a kitten that had lost its mother; she knew that her appearance was not attractive; she also had no sexual appeal. Finding a job? That was not for Sun Su. She lived in a small club, watching many giggling and romantic female stars float back and forth, and felt the envy and longing in her heart burning like fire. People pitied her and wanted to be her friend, but she was afraid and dared not look up. But a kind Mr. Francis Marin eventually gave her some work to do, making her a supporting actress for Mary Pickford. This was the first act of Sun Bici's film career.

This was really a blessing in Sun Su's life, because from that day on, she knew that there were people in the world who truly appreciated her, and she no longer doubted herself. At that time, Hollywood held a dance party every Thursday night. Sun Su attended the dance party for the first time and met Tom Gallely. Tom chose this Ms. Bici from among hundreds of beautiful girls. He asked her to dance. He said she had sexual appeal. Later, Ms. Bici married this Mr. Gallely. They lived a happy family life for several years. Unfortunately, Gallely's mood changed, and Bici suffered so much grievance that she couldn't bear it and divorced.

Sun Bici is a natural tragedian. Her nature tends towards bitterness; her views are also bitter; and she likes to listen to bitter stories. Once, the Hollywood night court asked about the deeds of a violated woman, and Sun Bici actually sat and listened all night. She herself said that she liked to listen to this naked statement of life's tragic circumstances. She can deeply empathize with those who feel the bitterness of life and the hunger of the soul.

But Sun Su's treatment of people and kisses is extremely sweet. The people of Hollywood have been praising Sun Bici's kindness to people. When the famous actress Barbara La Marr died, leaving behind a lonely and helpless adopted daughter, Sun Bici was moved with compassion and took the orphan over, making her feel no difference between her former mother and her stepmother. This is one of the widely praised deeds in Hollywood. (To be continued)

Local News

(1) Movie Actors Open Up New Avenues

— Yan

The sound film [Winning Glory for the Country] by Jinan Company, after filming the exterior scenes in Hangzhou, the interior scenes have invisibly stopped filming, supposedly because of a problem with the radio? This problem is also a money problem? So these actors wanted to find a way to make money during their spare time and organized a drama club for movie songs. Yesterday, they held a discussion meeting at the Central Film Trading Company and decided that the club would be called the "ISIS" [Oasis] Opera Society. It is said that singing star Li Lilian will participate, and Chen Dabei will write the script, Hu Xuguang will draw the scenery and design the stage set, the AClarins band, and eight dancers, Chen Gexin will guide the singing and score the music, Lu Fu and Gu Wenzong will direct, Wang Chunyuan and Chen Yitang will star, and Yangtianle will design the costumes, and Chen Baoqi will provide the lighting.

Today, Wang Naiding has already gone to Nanjing, Wuxi, and Suzhou to contact the theaters for the premiere. Shanghai will wait until the rehearsals are proficient before the premiere.

(2) The Return of the [Four Infantrymen]

— Muzhu

Shortly after the end of the Sino-Japanese war in Shanghai, a famous German war film that called itself an opposition to [All Quiet on the Western Front] was shown at the Carlton Theatre. Its name, which you have probably not forgotten, is [Four Infantrymen]. At that time, because the 19th Route Army retreated due to lack of reinforcements, the Japanese soldiers occupied many places, and everyone was so depressed that they wanted to watch war films to vent their anger. As a result, [Four Infantrymen] was very popular. As the saying goes, the venue was full and it was a sensation for a while.

It is said that [Four Infantrymen] will be re-released in Shanghai. In my opinion, it is still worth seeing. Movie fans in Hongkou, why not come and see it.

Movie Star Anecdotes

A Small History of Li Pingqian

— Lu Yasheng

Li Pingqian is a modern directing star, who transferred from Tianyi to Mingxing Company. He has many works, which I won't go into detail about; what I want to say now, I remember it was about seven or eight years ago! At this time, he was still studying at Jiaxing Xiuzhou Middle School, and I? But I was in the same school with him, but not in the same grade.

When he was in school, he was not very smart in his studies, but he was lively by nature, liked to move, not to be quiet, and was very fond of drama. Therefore, he did not score very high in his studies. I remember one semester, he was dismissed from school by the school authorities for failing mathematics. But he? He was not distressed or resentful, so he ran to Shanghai, and eventually entered the film company, and only then did he get to where he is now. Therefore, I remember when I was studying, I often heard the teachers say that no matter what you do, you should try your best to do it, don't be afraid to do it, and that failure is the mother of success, indeed.

I am not here to destroy Mr. Li's reputation, but I really admire his courage and give us a lesson. Although I am also on the road to art now, I still hope that Mr. Li will walk to the forefront.

Famous Works Translated

The Face of the Screen (Part 1)

— Translated by Dunruo

Qion Hanais Philipo, a filmmaker on a subway trip, accidentally looked up from the newspaper and saw the woman sitting across from him, which made his fingers cold. The woman's name was A Mai Telijiya Ersiji, you can't guess her age, she looks like an incarnation of sorrow. Not only did the pale and dull hair around her thin and depressed face frighten him, but the countless wrinkles on her face, the knotted hands on her bag, the worn shoes, and the patched clothes all deeply stimulated him. However, what inspired him the most was the extreme dullness, lifelessness, and despair in her eyes. He closed his eyes for a while, trying to get rid of the image she gave him, but in this instant, a creative idea arose very enthusiastically in his thoughts.

Suddenly, a crowd scene in a new film he was making, called [The Call of the Abyss], poured into his mind. He saw a group of black figures like the woman in front of him rushing up the stairs, and then one of them—the one sitting across from him now—left them alone, walking sadly a short distance separated from the crowd and the stairs. This group of frantic women pushed up behind her. He opened his eyes and realized that he was in the subway. He walked towards the woman and said in a half-loud voice:

[Would you like to see a Mr. written on this card? I think he can give you a good job.] His words stopped for a while before penetrating her senses. She still didn't look up, and finally she asked. [Is it odd jobs?]

[No, it's a very good job with a high salary. They will tell you the details when you get there.] [You know I have a job, 70 cents an hour every day, but this position will be gone. The office is closing soon. I like to do odd jobs.] (To be continued)

The picture below is a scene of Hu Die Xia Peizhen's jealousy and fight in [Flower of Freedom]. The film will be shown at the Nanjing Grand Theatre soon.

Fairy Tale Film

— Xiu Xi

[Flying Ambassador] (Air Mail Mystery) is a new product of Universal Company. The film is based on Western fairy tales and consists of twenty large volumes. These kinds of stories are almost exclusively for European and American children to watch. Therefore, the children in that country can tell you in detail! It is just like the children in our country, they can all tell fairy tales, [Flying Car], [Three Sisters], [Glass Shoes], etc., but, it is heard that the gentlemen of the Nanjing Film Inspection Committee have repeatedly re-examined it and still regard it as a suspicious case! In fact, fairy tales can be used by children for after-school entertainment, so the wise inspection gentlemen will definitely not regard the film as superstitious and absurd! Moreover, this kind of film is absolutely not absurd and preposterous! I think it will definitely pass in the shortest time, and at the same time, it can be used as entertainment for many children during Christmas! (Yet Reward)

Correction of Chen Yumei's Nickname

— Tianyi Contribution

Yesterday, this newspaper reported that Chen Yumei's nickname was Bao Bao, which is actually incorrect. Her original surname was Fei, and her nickname was Mengmin. Her father was the late famous doctor Fei Chunfu, who was the master of the Menghe School. When she was five years old, after her father passed away, she moved to Fei's villa in Suzhou City to grow up, so she can only speak Wu dialect softly. Later, she came to Shanghai at the age of fourteen and entered the film industry. People call her Bao Bao because of her young age, but it is not her nickname. At the age of sixteen, she transferred to Tianyi Company. At that time, Hu Die starred in the Pearl Tower film at Tianyi. She entered Tianyi to star in the Three Smiles film. The two films were completed one after another, and the business was better than other films. Therefore, their reputation gradually became known in the film industry. (Yet Reward)

Film Monograph

Conquering Yourself

— Chen Dabei

Plato once said, [The first and greatest victory is to conquer yourself; the person who is conquered by himself is the most shameful and base thing of all.]

I don't know if Plato has ever practiced performing arts or seen the process of training expressions. If he himself cannot express himself, then this sentence also includes himself. If he cannot be controlled by the environment and laugh when he wants to laugh and cry when he wants to cry, he himself is a person conquered by himself.

I have said repeatedly above that those who study performing arts should train the muscles of their faces to operate freely like drivers. To those who have no experience in the photography field, this is just a very plain and unremarkable sentence. Only after he tries it in front of the mirror will he know the value of this training. What is expression training? It is what Pala calls [Conquering yourself.]

If the muscles on your face are unwilling to be controlled by your will, the work of conquering yourself cannot be considered complete. For this reason, whether you want to make acting a career or not, you should use the time when you look at your face in the mirror to practice facial expressions. This is the last and most important work to complete your [Conquering yourself]. Except for those who intend to be hermits, facial expressions are something everyone should [learn and practice from time to time]. If the muscles on your face are not controlled by your mind, you will unknowingly suffer great losses! When you are talking, your heart is trying its best to express sincerity to the other party, but unfortunately your eyes are wandering there, showing a hesitant and doubtful attitude. What impression do you think the other party will have?
